ğŸ“ PUBLIC REVIEW:
The Cozy Cactus is indeed cozy ğŸ˜€. A spacious house that's tastefully decorated, refreshingly free of the usual cheap or chintzy furnishings found in other Airbnb rentals. It's well stocked with supplies.

Everything is well labeled so easy to find what we need. The hot tub was great with the cool weather.

Eann is a super host, very accommodating and helpful, and extremely responsive.  Average Response Time is given as one hour, but in reality, averaged less than a minute!

If you're planning to attend Coachella, and do things around La Quinta, Palm Desert, etc, this is a super location. We did a lot in Palm Springs and the drive was somewhat too long to be convenient (averaged 50 min to an hour)

Property is within a gated community so felt very safe. It has pools, fitness center and even pickleball courts. Getting in and out of the security gate was easy. We did not have any issues as shared in some reviews.

We had a great stay.

A few things that can use some improvements:
- the sliding glass doors and screens (from both kitchen and MBR) to the backyard are difficult to open and close. Something wrong with the sliding mechanism. 
- The smoker is great but would be easier and quicker with a gas grill.
- the hot tub is great and clean but water should be drained and tub refilled. It was very foamy from water not being changed out. Monitor indicated age of water!
- the curtain rod in MBR (by sliding glass door) kept falling down when we opened and closed curtains
- would be helpful to have more towel rods in bathrooms for wet towels
